<a id="tabsdata.tableframe.expr.expr.Expr.add"></a>
#### `add`

```python
def add(
    other: Any,
) -> Expr
```

[View source вҶ—](https://github.com/tabsdata/tabsdata/blob/b1.9/client/platform/src/main/python/tabsdata/tableframe/expr/expr.py#L196)

Equivalent to the + operator.

For numeric types adds the given input. For string types concatenates the given input.

**Categories:** numeric

**Parameters:**

<ParamField path="other" type="Any" required>
  The value to add or concatenate.
</ParamField>

#### Example

```python
>>> import tabsdata as td
>>>
>>> tf: td.TableFrame ...
>>>
>>> tf.select(td.col("val"), td.col("val").add(1).alias("add"))
>>>
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ val  в”Ҷ add      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ ---  в”Ҷ ---      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ i64  в”Ҷ i64      в”Ӯ
в•һв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Ў
в”Ӯ 1    в”Ҷ 2        в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 15   в”Ҷ 16       в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 18   в”Ҷ 19       в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 60   в”Ҷ 61       в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 60   в”Ҷ 61       в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 75   в”Ҷ 76       в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ null в”Ҷ null     в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
```

<a id="tabsdata.tableframe.expr.expr.Expr.alias"></a>
#### `alias`

```python
def alias(
    name: str,
) -> Expr
```

[View source вҶ—](https://github.com/tabsdata/tabsdata/blob/b1.9/client/platform/src/main/python/tabsdata/tableframe/expr/expr.py#L234)

Set the name for a column or expression.

**Categories:** manipulation

**Parameters:**

<ParamField path="name" type="str" required>
  Column or expression new name. The name must be a word ([A-Za-z_][A-Za-z0-9_]*) of up to 100 characters.
</ParamField>

#### Example

```python
>>> import tabsdata as td
>>>
>>> tf: td.TableFrame ...
>>>
>>> tf.select(td.col("age"), td.col("age").alias("Age"))
>>>
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ age  в”Ҷ Age  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ ---  в”Ҷ ---  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ i64  в”Ҷ i64  в”Ӯ
в•һв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Ў
в”Ӯ 1    в”Ҷ 1    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 15   в”Ҷ 15   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 18   в”Ҷ 18   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 60   в”Ҷ 60   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 60   в”Ҷ 60   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 75   в”Ҷ 75   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ null в”Ҷ null в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
```

<a id="tabsdata.tableframe.expr.expr.Expr.and_"></a>
#### `and_`

```python
def and_(
    * others: Any,
) -> Expr
```

[View source вҶ—](https://github.com/tabsdata/tabsdata/blob/b1.9/client/platform/src/main/python/tabsdata/tableframe/expr/expr.py#L270)

Bitwise and operator with the given expressions. It can be used with integer and bool types.

**Categories:** logic

**Parameters:**

<ParamField path="others" required>
  expressions to peform the bitwiseand with.
</ParamField>

#### Example

```python
>>> import tabsdata as td
>>>
>>> tf: td.TableFrame ...
>>>
>>> tf.select(td.col("i"), td.col("i").and_(2).alias("and_"))
>>>
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ i    в”Ҷ and_ в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ ---  в”Ҷ ---  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ i64  в”Ҷ i64  в”Ӯ
в•һв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Ў
в”Ӯ -1   в”Ҷ 2    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 2    в”Ҷ 2    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ -3   в”Ҷ 0    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 0    в”Ҷ 0    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 5    в”Ҷ 0    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 7    в”Ҷ 2    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ null в”Ҷ null в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
```

<a id="tabsdata.tableframe.expr.expr.Expr.cast"></a>
#### `cast`

```python
def cast(
    dtype: Boolean | Categorical | Date | Datetime | Decimal | Duration | Enum | Float16 | Float32 | Float64 | Int8 | Int16 | Int64 | Int32 | Int128 | Null | String | Time | UInt8 | UInt16 | UInt32 | UInt64 | type [ Any ],
    *,
    strict: bool = True,
    wrap_numerical: bool = False,
) -> Expr
```

[View source вҶ—](https://github.com/tabsdata/tabsdata/blob/b1.9/client/platform/src/main/python/tabsdata/tableframe/expr/expr.py#L492)

Cast a value to d different type.

**Categories:** type_casting

**Parameters:**

<ParamField path="dtype" type="Boolean | Categorical | Date | Datetime | Decimal | Duration | Enum | Float16 | Float32 | Float64 | Int8 | Int16 | Int64 | Int32 | Int128 | Null | String | Time | UInt8 | UInt16 | UInt32 | UInt64 | type [ Any ]" required>
  The data type to cast to.
</ParamField>

<ParamField path="strict" type="bool" default="True">
  If false, invalid casts produce nullвҖҷs; if true, an excetion is raised.
</ParamField>

<ParamField path="wrap_numerical" type="bool" default="False">
  If true, overflowing numbers ara handled; if false, an excetion is raised.
</ParamField>

#### Example

```python
>>> import tabsdata as td
>>> import polars as pl
>>>
>>> tf: td.TableFrame ...
>>>
>>> tf = tf.select(td.col("val"), td.col("val").cast(td.Float64)).alias("cast")
>>>
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ val  в”Ҷ cast в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ ---  в”Ҷ ---  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ i64  в”Ҷ f64  в”Ӯ
в•һв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Ў
в”Ӯ 1    в”Ҷ 1.0  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 15   в”Ҷ 15.0 в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 18   в”Ҷ 18.0 в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 60   в”Ҷ 60.0 в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 60   в”Ҷ 60.0 в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 75   в”Ҷ 75.0 в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ null в”Ҷ null в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
```

<a id="tabsdata.tableframe.expr.expr.Expr.ceil"></a>
#### `ceil`

```python
def ceil() -> Expr
```

[View source вҶ—](https://github.com/tabsdata/tabsdata/blob/b1.9/client/platform/src/main/python/tabsdata/tableframe/expr/expr.py#L571)

Round up the expression to the next integer value.

**Categories:** numeric

#### Example

```python
>>> import tabsdata as td
>>>
>>> tf: td.TableFrame ...
>>>
>>> tf = tf.select(td.col("temp"), td.col("temp").first().ceil().alias("ceil"))
>>>
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ temp в”Ҷ ceil    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ ---  в”Ҷ ------- в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ f64  в”Ҷ f64     в”Ӯ
в•һв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Ў
в”Ӯ 1.0  в”Ҷ  1.0    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 1.1  в”Ҷ  2.0    в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
```

<a id="tabsdata.tableframe.expr.expr.Expr.clip"></a>
#### `clip`

```python
def clip(
    lower_bound: int | float | Decimal | date | time | datetime | timedelta | Expr | Series | str | None = None,
    upper_bound: int | float | Decimal | date | time | datetime | timedelta | Expr | Series | str | None = None,
) -> Expr
```

[View source вҶ—](https://github.com/tabsdata/tabsdata/blob/b1.9/client/platform/src/main/python/tabsdata/tableframe/expr/expr.py#L597)

For element values outside the lower and upper bounds, lower values are replaced with the lower bound and upper values with the upper bound. Values within the lower and upper bounds are unaffected.

**Categories:** numeric

**Parameters:**

<ParamField path="lower_bound" type="int | float | Decimal | date | time | datetime | timedelta | Expr | Series | str | None" default="None">
  The lower bound value. If None, the lower bound is not set.
</ParamField>

<ParamField path="upper_bound" type="int | float | Decimal | date | time | datetime | timedelta | Expr | Series | str | None" default="None">
  The upper bound value. If None, the upper bound is
</ParamField>

#### Example

```python
>>> import tabsdata as td
>>>
>>> tf: td.TableFrame ...
>>>
>>> tf = tf.select(td.col("age"), td.col("age").clip(18,65).alias("clip"))
>>>
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ age  в”Ҷ clip    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ ---  в”Ҷ ------- в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ i64  в”Ҷ i64     в”Ӯ
в•һв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җ+++в•җв•җв•җв•Ў
в”Ӯ 1    в”Ҷ 18      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 18   в”Ҷ 18      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 50   в”Ҷ 50      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 65   в”Ҷ 65      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 70   в”Ҷ 65      в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
```

```python
в”Ӯ ---  в”Ҷ ---  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ str  в”Ҷ i64  в”Ӯ
в•һв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Ў

в”Ӯ B    в”Ҷ 0    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ C    в”Ҷ 5    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ null в”Ҷ 6    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ C    в”Ҷ null в”Ӯ

>>> tf.group_by(td.col("a")).agg(td.col("b")).count().alias("count"))
>>>

в”Ӯ C    в”Ҷ 1     в”Ӯ
```

```python
    other: Any,
```

[View source вҶ—](https://github.com/tabsdata/tabsdata/blob/b1.9/client/platform/src/main/python/tabsdata/tableframe/expr/expr.py#L777)

Compare if 2 expressions are equal, equivalent to expr == other. If one of the expressions is null (None) it returns null.

</ParamField>

```python
в”Ӯ f64 в”Ҷ f64  в”Ҷ bool  в”Ӯ

в”Ӯ 2.0 в”Ҷ 2.0  в”Ҷ true  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ NaN в”Ҷ NaN  в”Ҷ true  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 4.0 в”Ҷ NaN  в”Ҷ false в”Ӯ
```

<a id="tabsdata.tableframe.expr.expr.Expr.fill_null"></a>
#### `fill_null`

```python
def fill_null(
    value: Any | Expr | None = None,
    strategy: Literal [ 'forward' , 'backward' , 'min' , 'max' , 'mean' , 'zero' , 'one' ] | None = None,
    limit: int | None = None,
) -> Expr
```

[View source вҶ—](https://github.com/tabsdata/tabsdata/blob/b1.9/client/platform/src/main/python/tabsdata/tableframe/expr/expr.py#L910)

Replace null values with the given value.

**Categories:** manipulation

**Parameters:**

<ParamField path="value" type="Any | Expr | None" default="None">
  The value to replacenull values with.
</ParamField>

<ParamField path="strategy" type="Literal [ 'forward' , 'backward' , 'min' , 'max' , 'mean' , 'zero' , 'one' ] | None" default="None">
  The strategy to use for fillingnull values.
</ParamField>

<ParamField path="limit" type="int | None" default="None">
  The maximum number ofnull values to replace.
</ParamField>

#### Example

```python
>>> import tabsdata as td
>>>
>>> tf: td.TableFrame ...
>>>
>>> tf = tf.select(td.col("val"), td.col("val")
>>>        .fill_null(5.5).alias("fill_null"))
>>>
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ val  в”Ҷ fill_null в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ ---  в”Ҷ ---       в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ f64  в”Ҷ f64       в”Ӯ
в•һв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Ў
в”Ӯ -1.0 в”Ҷ -1.0      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 0.0  в”Ҷ 0.0       в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 1.1  в”Ҷ 1.1       в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 2.0  в”Ҷ 2.0       в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ inf  в”Ҷ inf       в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ null в”Ҷ 5.5       в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ NaN  в”Ҷ NaN       в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
```

<a id="tabsdata.tableframe.expr.expr.Expr.filter"></a>
#### `filter`

```python
def filter(
    * predicates: Expr | Series | str | Iterable [ Expr | Series | str ],
) -> Expr
```

[View source вҶ—](https://github.com/tabsdata/tabsdata/blob/b1.9/client/platform/src/main/python/tabsdata/tableframe/expr/expr.py#L957)

Apply a filter predicate to an expression.

Elements for which the predicate does not evaluate to true are discarded, evaluations to null are also discarded.

Useful in an aggregation expression.

**Categories:** filters

**Parameters:**

<ParamField path="predicates" required>
  Expression(s) that evaluates to a boolean.
</ParamField>

#### Example

```python
>>> import tabsdata as td
>>>
>>> tf: td.TableFrame ...
>>>
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ state в”Ҷ tickets в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ ---   в”Ҷ ---     в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ str   в”Ҷ i64     в”Ӯ
в•һв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Ў
в”Ӯ CA    в”Ҷ 1       в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ AL    в”Ҷ 3       в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ CA    в”Ҷ 2       в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ NY    в”Ҷ 2       в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ NY    в”Ҷ 3       в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
>>>
>>> import tabsdata as td
>>> tf.group_by("state").agg(td.col("tickets")
>>>   .filter(td.col("tickets") !=2)
>>>   .sum().alias("sum_non_two"))
>>>
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ state в”Ҷ sum_non_two в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ ---   в”Ҷ ---         в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ str   в”Ҷ i64         в”Ӯ
в•һв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Ў
в”Ӯ AL    в”Ҷ 3           в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ NY    в”Ҷ 3           в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ CA    в”Ҷ 1           в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
```

```python
в”Ӯ 2.0  в”Ҷ 4738789230185236462 в”Ӯ
```

<a id="tabsdata.tableframe.expr.expr.Expr.is_between"></a>
#### `is_between`

```python
def is_between(
    lower_bound: td_typing.IntoExpr,
    upper_bound: td_typing.IntoExpr,
    closed: td_typing.ClosedInterval = 'both',
) -> Expr
```

[View source вҶ—](https://github.com/tabsdata/tabsdata/blob/b1.9/client/platform/src/main/python/tabsdata/tableframe/expr/expr.py#L1194)

If an expression is between the given bounds.

**Categories:** logic

**Parameters:**

<ParamField path="lower_bound" type="td_typing.IntoExpr" required>
  The lower bound value.
</ParamField>

<ParamField path="upper_bound" type="td_typing.IntoExpr" required>
  The upper bound value.
</ParamField>

<ParamField path="closed" type="td_typing.ClosedInterval" default="'both'">
  The interval type, either вҖңbothвҖқ, вҖңleftвҖқ, вҖңrightвҖқ, or вҖңneitherвҖқ
</ParamField>

#### Example

```python
>>> import tabsdata as td
>>>
>>> tf: td.TableFrame ...
>>>
>>> tf = tf.select(td.col("temp"), td.col("temp")
>>> .is_between(0, 1).alias("between"))
>>>
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ

в”Ӯ f64  в”Ҷ bool    в”Ӯ
в•һв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Ў
в”Ӯ-1.0  в”Ҷ  false  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 0.0  в”Ҷ  true   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 0.5  в”Ҷ  true   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 1.0  в”Ҷ  true   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 1.1  в”Ҷ  false  в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
```

```python
в”Ӯ 1.1  в”Ҷ true     в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ Nan  в”Ҷ false    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ None в”Ҷ false    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ inf  в”Ҷ true     в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
```

<a id="tabsdata.tableframe.expr.expr.Expr.len"></a>
#### `len`

```python
def len() -> Expr
```

[View source вҶ—](https://github.com/tabsdata/tabsdata/blob/b1.9/client/platform/src/main/python/tabsdata/tableframe/expr/expr.py#L2316)

Aggregation operation that counts the rows in the group.

**Categories:** aggregation

#### Examples

```python
>>> import tabsdata as td
>>>
>>> tf: td.TableFrame ...
>>>
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ a    в”Ҷ b    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ ---  в”Ҷ ---  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ str  в”Ҷ i64  в”Ӯ
в•һв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Ў
в”Ӯ A    в”Ҷ 1    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ B    в”Ҷ 2    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ A    в”Ҷ 3    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ B    в”Ҷ 0    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ C    в”Ҷ 5    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ null в”Ҷ 6    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ C    в”Ҷ null в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
>>>
>>> tf.group_by(td.col("a")).agg(td.col("b")).len().alias("len"))
>>>
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ a    в”Ҷ len в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ ---  в”Ҷ --- в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ str  в”Ҷ u32 в”Ӯ
в•һв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Ў
в”Ӯ null в”Ҷ 1   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ A    в”Ҷ 2   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ B    в”Ҷ 2   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ C    в”Ҷ 2   в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
```

[View source вҶ—](https://github.com/tabsdata/tabsdata/blob/b1.9/client/platform/src/main/python/tabsdata/tableframe/expr/expr.py#L2472)

```python
def mean() -> Expr
```

[View source вҶ—](https://github.com/tabsdata/tabsdata/blob/b1.9/client/platform/src/main/python/tabsdata/tableframe/expr/expr.py#L2616)

Aggregation operation that finds the mean of the values in the group.

#### Examples

```python
>>> import tabsdata as td
>>>
>>> tf: td.TableFrame ...
>>>
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ ss   в”Ҷ i    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ ---  в”Ҷ ---  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ str  в”Ҷ i64  в”Ӯ
в•һв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Ў
в”Ӯ A    в”Ҷ 1    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ B    в”Ҷ 0    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ A    в”Ҷ 2    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ B    в”Ҷ 3    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ B    в”Ҷ 4    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ C    в”Ҷ -1   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ C    в”Ҷ -2   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ C    в”Ҷ -3   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ D    в”Ҷ -4   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ F    в”Ҷ -5   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ null в”Ҷ null в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
>>>
>>> tf.group_by(td.col("a")).agg(td.col("b").mean())
>>>
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ ss   в”Ҷ i        в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ ---  в”Ҷ ---      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ str  в”Ҷ f64      в”Ӯ
в•һв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Ў
в”Ӯ null в”Ҷ null     в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ A    в”Ҷ 1.5      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ F    в”Ҷ -5.0     в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ C    в”Ҷ -2.0     в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ D    в”Ҷ -4.0     в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ B    в”Ҷ 2.333333 в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
```

[View source вҶ—](https://github.com/tabsdata/tabsdata/blob/b1.9/client/platform/src/main/python/tabsdata/tableframe/expr/expr.py#L2664)

**Categories:** aggregation

#### Examples

```python

>>>
>>> tf: td.TableFrame ...

в”Ӯ B    в”Ҷ 0    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ A    в”Ҷ 2    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ B    в”Ҷ 3    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ B    в”Ҷ 4    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ C    в”Ҷ -1   в”Ӯ

в”Ӯ C    в”Ҷ -3   в”Ӯ

в”Ӯ F    в”Ҷ -5   в”Ӯ

в”Ӯ D    в”Ҷ -4.0 в”Ӯ
```

<a id="tabsdata.tableframe.expr.expr.Expr.ne"></a>
#### `ne`

```python
def ne(
    other: Any,
) -> Expr
```

[View source вҶ—](https://github.com/tabsdata/tabsdata/blob/b1.9/client/platform/src/main/python/tabsdata/tableframe/expr/expr.py#L1723)

Compare if 2 expressions are not equal, equivalent to expr != other. If one of the expressions is null (None) it returns null.

**Categories:** logic

**Parameters:**

<ParamField path="other" type="Any" required>
  The value to compare with.
</ParamField>

#### Example

```python
>>> import tabsdata as td
>>>
>>> tf: td.TableFrame ...
>>>
>>> tf = tf.select(td.col("a").ne(td.col("b")).alias("ne"))
>>>
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ a   в”Ҷ b    в”Ҷ ne    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ --- в”Ҷ ---  в”Ҷ ---   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ f64 в”Ҷ f64  в”Ҷ bool  в”Ӯ
в•һв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Ў
в”Ӯ 1.0 в”Ҷ 2.0  в”Ҷ true  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 2.0 в”Ҷ 2.0  в”Ҷ false в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ NaN в”Ҷ NaN  в”Ҷ false в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 4.0 в”Ҷ NaN  в”Ҷ true  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 5.0 в”Ҷ null в”Ҷ null  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ nullв”Ҷ null в”Ҷ null  в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
```

<a id="tabsdata.tableframe.expr.expr.Expr.ne_missing"></a>
#### `ne_missing`

```python
def ne_missing(
    other: Any,
) -> Expr
```

[View source вҶ—](https://github.com/tabsdata/tabsdata/blob/b1.9/client/platform/src/main/python/tabsdata/tableframe/expr/expr.py#L1758)

Compare if 2 expressions are not equal an, equivalent to expr != other. If one of the expressions is null (None) it returns false.

**Categories:** logic

**Parameters:**

<ParamField path="other" type="Any" required>
  The value to compare with.
</ParamField>

#### Example

```python
>>> import tabsdata as td
>>>
>>> tf: td.TableFrame ...
>>>
>>> tf = tf.select(td.col("a").eq(td.col("b")).alias("ne_missing"))
>>>

в”Ӯ a   в”Ҷ b    в”Ҷ ne_missingв”Ӯ
в”Ӯ --- в”Ҷ ---  в”Ҷ ---       в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ f64 в”Ҷ f64  в”Ҷ bool      в”Ӯ
в•һв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Ў
в”Ӯ 1.0 в”Ҷ 2.0  в”Ҷ true      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 2.0 в”Ҷ 2.0  в”Ҷ false     в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ NaN в”Ҷ NaN  в”Ҷ false     в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 4.0 в”Ҷ NaN  в”Ҷ true      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 5.0 в”Ҷ null в”Ҷ true      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ nullв”Ҷ null в”Ҷ false     в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
```

<a id="tabsdata.tableframe.expr.expr.Expr.radians"></a>
#### `radians`

```python
def radians() -> Expr
```

[View source вҶ—](https://github.com/tabsdata/tabsdata/blob/b1.9/client/platform/src/main/python/tabsdata/tableframe/expr/expr.py#L1918)

Convert a degree value to radians

**Categories:** numeric

#### Example

```python
>>> import tabsdata as td
>>>
>>> tf: td.TableFrame ...
>>>
>>> tf = tf.select(td.col("val"), td.col("val").radians().alias("radians"))
>>>
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ val     в”Ҷ radians  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ ---     в”Ҷ ---      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ i64     в”Ҷ f64      в”Ӯ
в•һв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Ў
в”Ӯ 1       в”Ҷ 0.017453 в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 15      в”Ҷ 0.261799 в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 60      в”Ҷ 1.047198 в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 75      в”Ҷ 1.308997 в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ null    в”Ҷ null     в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
```

<a id="tabsdata.tableframe.expr.expr.Expr.rank"></a>
#### `rank`

```python
def rank(
    method: Literal [ 'average' , 'min' , 'max' , 'dense' , 'ordinal' , 'random' ] = 'average',
    *,
    descending: bool = False,
    seed: int | None = None,
) -> Expr
```

[View source вҶ—](https://github.com/tabsdata/tabsdata/blob/b1.9/client/platform/src/main/python/tabsdata/tableframe/expr/expr.py#L1947)

Compute the rank of the element values. Multiple rank types are available.

**Categories:** aggregation

**Parameters:**

<ParamField path="method" type="Literal [ 'average' , 'min' , 'max' , 'dense' , 'ordinal' , 'random' ]" default="'average'">
  the ranking type: вҖҳaverageвҖҷ (default), вҖҳdenseвҖҷ, вҖҳmaxвҖҷ, вҖҳminвҖҷ, вҖҳordinalвҖҷ or вҖҳrandomвҖҷ.
</ParamField>

<ParamField path="descending" type="bool" default="False">
  if the order is ascending (default) or descending.
</ParamField>

<ParamField path="seed" type="int | None" default="None">
  random seed when using вҖҳrandomвҖҷ rank type.
</ParamField>

#### Example

```python
>>> import tabsdata as td
>>>
>>> tf: td.TableFrame ...
>>>
>>> tf.select(td.col("val"), td.col("val").rank("max").alias("rank"))
>>>
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ val  в”Ҷ rank в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ ---  в”Ҷ ---  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ f64  в”Ҷ u32  в”Ӯ
в•һв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Ў
в”Ӯ -1.0 в”Ҷ 1    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 0.0  в”Ҷ 2    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 1.1  в”Ҷ 3    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 2.0  в”Ҷ 4    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ inf  в”Ҷ 5    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ null в”Ҷ null в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ NaN  в”Ҷ 6    в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
```

<a id="tabsdata.tableframe.expr.expr.Expr.reinterpret"></a>
#### `reinterpret`

```python
def reinterpret(
    *,
    signed: bool = True,
) -> Expr
```

[View source вҶ—](https://github.com/tabsdata/tabsdata/blob/b1.9/client/platform/src/main/python/tabsdata/tableframe/expr/expr.py#L2034)

Reinterpret the 64bit element values (i64 or u64) as a signed/unsigned integers. Only valid for 64bit integers, for other types use cast.

**Categories:** numeric

**Parameters:**

<ParamField path="signed" type="bool" default="True">
  true to convert to i64, false to convert to u64. This named argument must be specified.
</ParamField>

#### Example

```python
>>> import tabsdata as td
>>>
>>> tf: td.TableFrame ...
>>>
>>> tf.select(td.col("val"), td.col("val")
>>>   .reinterpret(signed=False).alias("reinterpret"))
>>>
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ val  в”Ҷ reinterpret в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ ---  в”Ҷ ---         в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ i64  в”Ҷ u64         в”Ӯ
в•һв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Ў
в”Ӯ 3    в”Ҷ 3           в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 1    в”Ҷ 1           в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 5    в”Ҷ 5           в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 4    в”Ҷ 4           в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 2    в”Ҷ 2           в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 6    в”Ҷ 6           в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ null в”Ҷ null        в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
```

```python
в•һв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Ў
в”Ӯ A    в”Ҷ 1    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ B    в”Ҷ 0    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ A    в”Ҷ 2    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ B    в”Ҷ 3    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ B    в”Ҷ 4    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ C    в”Ҷ -1   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ C    в”Ҷ -2   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ C    в”Ҷ -3   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ D    в”Ҷ -4   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ F    в”Ҷ -5   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ null в”Ҷ null в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
>>>
>>> tf.group_by(td.col("a")).agg(td.col("b")).sum())
>>>
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ ss   в”Ҷ i   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ ---  в”Ҷ --- в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ str  в”Ҷ i64 в”Ӯ
в•һв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Ў
в”Ӯ null в”Ҷ 0   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ A    в”Ҷ 3   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ B    в”Ҷ 7   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ C    в”Ҷ -6  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ D    в”Ҷ -4  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ F    в”Ҷ -5  в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
```

```python
в”Ӯ 0.6  в”Ҷ 0.54042  в”Ӯ
```

<summary>cast</summary>


```python
def cast(
    dtype: Boolean | Categorical | Date | Datetime | Decimal | Duration | Enum | Float16 | Float32 | Float64 | Int8 | Int16 | Int64 | Int32 | Int128 | Null | String | Time | UInt8 | UInt16 | UInt32 | UInt64 | type [ Any ],
    *,
    strict: bool = True,
    wrap_numerical: bool = False,
) -> Expr
```

[View source вҶ—](https://github.com/tabsdata/tabsdata/blob/b1.9/client/platform/src/main/python/tabsdata/tableframe/expr/expr.py#L492)

Cast a value to d different type.

**Categories:** type_casting

**Parameters:**

<ParamField path="dtype" type="Boolean | Categorical | Date | Datetime | Decimal | Duration | Enum | Float16 | Float32 | Float64 | Int8 | Int16 | Int64 | Int32 | Int128 | Null | String | Time | UInt8 | UInt16 | UInt32 | UInt64 | type [ Any ]" required>
  The data type to cast to.
</ParamField>

<ParamField path="strict" type="bool" default="True">
  If false, invalid casts produce nullвҖҷs; if true, an excetion is raised.
</ParamField>

<ParamField path="wrap_numerical" type="bool" default="False">
  If true, overflowing numbers ara handled; if false, an excetion is raised.
</ParamField>

#### Example

```python
>>> import tabsdata as td
>>> import polars as pl
>>>
>>> tf: td.TableFrame ...
>>>
>>> tf = tf.select(td.col("val"), td.col("val").cast(td.Float64)).alias("cast")
>>>

в”Ӯ 18   в”Ҷ 18.0 в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 60   в”Ҷ 60.0 в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 60   в”Ҷ 60.0 в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 75   в”Ҷ 75.0 в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ null в”Ҷ null в”Ӯ
```

<a id="id14"></a>
<details>
<summary>clip</summary>


```python
def clip(
    lower_bound: int | float | Decimal | date | time | datetime | timedelta | Expr | Series | str | None = None,
    upper_bound: int | float | Decimal | date | time | datetime | timedelta | Expr | Series | str | None = None,
) -> Expr
```

[View source вҶ—](https://github.com/tabsdata/tabsdata/blob/b1.9/client/platform/src/main/python/tabsdata/tableframe/expr/expr.py#L597)

For element values outside the lower and upper bounds, lower values are replaced with the lower bound and upper values with the upper bound. Values within the lower and upper bounds are unaffected.

**Categories:** numeric

**Parameters:**

<ParamField path="lower_bound" type="int | float | Decimal | date | time | datetime | timedelta | Expr | Series | str | None" default="None">
  The lower bound value. If None, the lower bound is not set.
</ParamField>

<ParamField path="upper_bound" type="int | float | Decimal | date | time | datetime | timedelta | Expr | Series | str | None" default="None">
  The upper bound value. If None, the upper bound is
</ParamField>

#### Example

```python
>>> import tabsdata as td
>>>
>>> tf: td.TableFrame ...
>>>
>>> tf = tf.select(td.col("age"), td.col("age").clip(18,65).alias("clip"))
>>>
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ age  в”Ҷ clip    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ ---  в”Ҷ ------- в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ i64  в”Ҷ i64     в”Ӯ
в•һв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җ+++в•җв•җв•җв•Ў
в”Ӯ 1    в”Ҷ 18      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 18   в”Ҷ 18      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 50   в”Ҷ 50      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 65   в”Ҷ 65      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 70   в”Ҷ 65      в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
```

```python
>>>
```

```python
def diff(
    n: int = 1,
) -> Expr
```

[View source вҶ—](https://github.com/tabsdata/tabsdata/blob/b1.9/client/platform/src/main/python/tabsdata/tableframe/expr/expr.py#L1990)

Compute the difference between an element value and the element value of the specified relative row.

It supports numberic and datetime types.

**Categories:** numeric

**Parameters:**

<ParamField path="n" type="int" default="1">
  The relative row to compute the difference with. Defaults to 1 (previous). Use a negative number to get a next row.
</ParamField>

```python
>>>

в”Ӯ 3    в”Ҷ 1    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 4    в”Ҷ 1    в”Ӯ

в”Ӯ -2   в”Ҷ -1   в”Ӯ
```

<a id="id21"></a>
<details>
<summary>eq</summary>


```python
def eq(
    other: Any,
) -> Expr
```

[View source вҶ—](https://github.com/tabsdata/tabsdata/blob/b1.9/client/platform/src/main/python/tabsdata/tableframe/expr/expr.py#L777)

Compare if 2 expressions are equal, equivalent to expr == other. If one of the expressions is null (None) it returns null.

**Categories:** logic

**Parameters:**

<ParamField path="other" type="Any" required>
  The value to compare with.
</ParamField>

#### Example

```python
>>> import tabsdata as td
>>>
>>> tf: td.TableFrame ...
>>>
>>> tf = tf.select(td.col("a").eq(td.col("b")).alias("eq"))
>>>
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ a   в”Ҷ b    в”Ҷ eq    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ --- в”Ҷ ---  в”Ҷ ---   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ f64 в”Ҷ f64  в”Ҷ bool  в”Ӯ
в•һв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Ў
в”Ӯ 1.0 в”Ҷ 2.0  в”Ҷ false в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 2.0 в”Ҷ 2.0  в”Ҷ true  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ NaN в”Ҷ NaN  в”Ҷ true  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 4.0 в”Ҷ NaN  в”Ҷ false в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 5.0 в”Ҷ null в”Ҷ null  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ nullв”Ҷ null в”Ҷ null  в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
```

<a id="id26"></a>
<details>
<summary>filter</summary>


```python
def filter(
    * predicates: Expr | Series | str | Iterable [ Expr | Series | str ],
) -> Expr
```

[View source вҶ—](https://github.com/tabsdata/tabsdata/blob/b1.9/client/platform/src/main/python/tabsdata/tableframe/expr/expr.py#L957)

Apply a filter predicate to an expression.

Elements for which the predicate does not evaluate to true are discarded, evaluations to null are also discarded.

Useful in an aggregation expression.

**Categories:** filters

**Parameters:**

<ParamField path="predicates" required>
  Expression(s) that evaluates to a boolean.
</ParamField>

#### Example

```python
>>> import tabsdata as td
>>>
>>> tf: td.TableFrame ...
>>>
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ state в”Ҷ tickets в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ ---   в”Ҷ ---     в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ str   в”Ҷ i64     в”Ӯ
в•һв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Ў
в”Ӯ CA    в”Ҷ 1       в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ AL    в”Ҷ 3       в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ CA    в”Ҷ 2       в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ NY    в”Ҷ 2       в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ NY    в”Ҷ 3       в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
>>>
>>> import tabsdata as td
>>> tf.group_by("state").agg(td.col("tickets")
>>>   .filter(td.col("tickets") !=2)
>>>   .sum().alias("sum_non_two"))
>>>
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ state в”Ҷ sum_non_two в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ ---   в”Ҷ ---         в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ str   в”Ҷ i64         в”Ӯ
в•һв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Ў
в”Ӯ AL    в”Ҷ 3           в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ NY    в”Ҷ 3           в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ CA    в”Ҷ 1           в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
```

<a id="id33"></a>
<details>
<summary>is_between</summary>


```python
def is_between(
    lower_bound: td_typing.IntoExpr,
    upper_bound: td_typing.IntoExpr,
    closed: td_typing.ClosedInterval = 'both',
) -> Expr
```

[View source вҶ—](https://github.com/tabsdata/tabsdata/blob/b1.9/client/platform/src/main/python/tabsdata/tableframe/expr/expr.py#L1194)

If an expression is between the given bounds.

**Categories:** logic

**Parameters:**

<ParamField path="lower_bound" type="td_typing.IntoExpr" required>
  The lower bound value.
</ParamField>

<ParamField path="upper_bound" type="td_typing.IntoExpr" required>
  The upper bound value.
</ParamField>

<ParamField path="closed" type="td_typing.ClosedInterval" default="'both'">
  The interval type, either вҖңbothвҖқ, вҖңleftвҖқ, вҖңrightвҖқ, or вҖңneitherвҖқ
</ParamField>

#### Example

```python
>>> import tabsdata as td
>>>
>>> tf: td.TableFrame ...
>>>
>>> tf = tf.select(td.col("temp"), td.col("temp")
>>> .is_between(0, 1).alias("between"))
>>>
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ temp в”Ҷ between в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ ---  в”Ҷ ------- в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ f64  в”Ҷ bool    в”Ӯ
в•һв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Ў
в”Ӯ-1.0  в”Ҷ  false  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 0.0  в”Ҷ  true   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 0.5  в”Ҷ  true   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 1.0  в”Ҷ  true   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 1.1  в”Ҷ  false  в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
```

```python
def len() -> Expr
```

[View source вҶ—](https://github.com/tabsdata/tabsdata/blob/b1.9/client/platform/src/main/python/tabsdata/tableframe/expr/expr.py#L2316)

Aggregation operation that counts the rows in the group.

**Categories:** aggregation

#### Examples

```python
>>> import tabsdata as td
>>>
>>> tf: td.TableFrame ...
>>>
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ a    в”Ҷ b    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ ---  в”Ҷ ---  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ str  в”Ҷ i64  в”Ӯ
в•һв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Ў
в”Ӯ A    в”Ҷ 1    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ B    в”Ҷ 2    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ A    в”Ҷ 3    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ B    в”Ҷ 0    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ C    в”Ҷ 5    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ null в”Ҷ 6    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ C    в”Ҷ null в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
>>>
>>> tf.group_by(td.col("a")).agg(td.col("b")).len().alias("len"))
>>>
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ a    в”Ҷ len в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ ---  в”Ҷ --- в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ str  в”Ҷ u32 в”Ӯ
в•һв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Ў
в”Ӯ null в”Ҷ 1   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ A    в”Ҷ 2   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ B    в”Ҷ 2   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ C    в”Ҷ 2   в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
```

```python
в”Ӯ null в”Ҷ null     в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ NaN  в”Ҷ NaN      в”Ӯ
```

<a id="id56"></a>
<details>
<summary>ne</summary>


```python
def ne(
    other: Any,
) -> Expr
```

[View source вҶ—](https://github.com/tabsdata/tabsdata/blob/b1.9/client/platform/src/main/python/tabsdata/tableframe/expr/expr.py#L1723)

Compare if 2 expressions are not equal, equivalent to expr != other. If one of the expressions is null (None) it returns null.

**Categories:** logic

**Parameters:**

<ParamField path="other" type="Any" required>
  The value to compare with.
</ParamField>

#### Example

```python
>>> import tabsdata as td
>>>
>>> tf: td.TableFrame ...
>>>
>>> tf = tf.select(td.col("a").ne(td.col("b")).alias("ne"))
>>>
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ a   в”Ҷ b    в”Ҷ ne    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ --- в”Ҷ ---  в”Ҷ ---   в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ f64 в”Ҷ f64  в”Ҷ bool  в”Ӯ
в•һв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Ў
в”Ӯ 1.0 в”Ҷ 2.0  в”Ҷ true  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 2.0 в”Ҷ 2.0  в”Ҷ false в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ NaN в”Ҷ NaN  в”Ҷ false в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 4.0 в”Ҷ NaN  в”Ҷ true  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 5.0 в”Ҷ null в”Ҷ null  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ nullв”Ҷ null в”Ҷ null  в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
```


</details>

<a id="id57"></a>
<details>
<summary>ne_missing</summary>


```python
def ne_missing(
    other: Any,
) -> Expr
```

[View source вҶ—](https://github.com/tabsdata/tabsdata/blob/b1.9/client/platform/src/main/python/tabsdata/tableframe/expr/expr.py#L1758)

Compare if 2 expressions are not equal an, equivalent to expr != other. If one of the expressions is null (None) it returns false.

**Categories:** logic

**Parameters:**

<ParamField path="other" type="Any" required>
  The value to compare with.
</ParamField>

#### Example

```python
>>> import tabsdata as td
>>>
>>> tf: td.TableFrame ...
>>>
>>> tf = tf.select(td.col("a").eq(td.col("b")).alias("ne_missing"))
>>>
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ a   в”Ҷ b    в”Ҷ ne_missingв”Ӯ
в”Ӯ --- в”Ҷ ---  в”Ҷ ---       в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ f64 в”Ҷ f64  в”Ҷ bool      в”Ӯ
в•һв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Ў
в”Ӯ 1.0 в”Ҷ 2.0  в”Ҷ true      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 2.0 в”Ҷ 2.0  в”Ҷ false     в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ NaN в”Ҷ NaN  в”Ҷ false     в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 4.0 в”Ҷ NaN  в”Ҷ true      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 5.0 в”Ҷ null в”Ҷ true      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ nullв”Ҷ null в”Ҷ false     в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
```

<summary>rank</summary>


```python
def rank(
    method: Literal [ 'average' , 'min' , 'max' , 'dense' , 'ordinal' , 'random' ] = 'average',
    *,
    descending: bool = False,
    seed: int | None = None,
) -> Expr
```

[View source вҶ—](https://github.com/tabsdata/tabsdata/blob/b1.9/client/platform/src/main/python/tabsdata/tableframe/expr/expr.py#L1947)

Compute the rank of the element values. Multiple rank types are available.

**Categories:** aggregation

**Parameters:**

<ParamField path="method" type="Literal [ 'average' , 'min' , 'max' , 'dense' , 'ordinal' , 'random' ]" default="'average'">
  the ranking type: вҖҳaverageвҖҷ (default), вҖҳdenseвҖҷ, вҖҳmaxвҖҷ, вҖҳminвҖҷ, вҖҳordinalвҖҷ or вҖҳrandomвҖҷ.
</ParamField>

<ParamField path="descending" type="bool" default="False">
  if the order is ascending (default) or descending.
</ParamField>

<ParamField path="seed" type="int | None" default="None">
  random seed when using вҖҳrandomвҖҷ rank type.
</ParamField>

#### Example

```python
>>> import tabsdata as td
>>>
>>> tf: td.TableFrame ...
>>>
>>> tf.select(td.col("val"), td.col("val").rank("max").alias("rank"))
>>>
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ val  в”Ҷ rank в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ ---  в”Ҷ ---  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ f64  в”Ҷ u32  в”Ӯ
в•һв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Әв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•Ў
в”Ӯ -1.0 в”Ҷ 1    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 0.0  в”Ҷ 2    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 1.1  в”Ҷ 3    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ 2.0  в”Ҷ 4    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ inf  в”Ҷ 5    в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ null в”Ҷ null в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ NaN  в”Ҷ 6    в”Ӯ
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
```

<a id="tabsdata.tableframe.expr.expr.P"></a>
<details>
<summary>P</summary>


Parameter specification variable.

The preferred way to construct a parameter specification is via the dedicated syntax for generic functions, classes, and type aliases, where the use of вҖҳ**вҖҷ creates a parameter specification:

```python
type IntFunc[**P] = Callable[P, int]
```

```python
P = ParamSpec('P')
```

```python
def add_logging[**P, T](f: Callable[P, T]) -> Callable[P, T]:
    '''A type-safe decorator to add logging to a function.'''
    def inner(*args: P.args, **kwargs: P.kwargs) -> T:
        logging.info(f'{f.__name__} was called')
        return f(*args, **kwargs)
    return inner

@add_logging
def add_two(x: float, y: float) -> float:
    '''Add two numbers together.'''
    return x + y
```

```python
>>> P = ParamSpec("P")
>>> P.__name__
'P'
```


</details>

<a id="tabsdata.tableframe.expr.expr.T"></a>
<details>
<summary>T</summary>


Type variable.

The preferred way to construct a type variable is via the dedicated syntax for generic functions, classes, and type aliases:

```python
class Sequence[T]:  # T is a TypeVar
    ...
```

```python
# S is a TypeVar bound to str
class StrSequence[S: str]:
    ...

# A is a TypeVar constrained to str or bytes
class StrOrBytesSequence[A: (str, bytes)]:
    ...
```

```python
T = TypeVar('T')  # Can be anything
S = TypeVar('S', bound=str)  # Can be any subtype of str
A = TypeVar('A', str, bytes)  # Must be exactly str or bytes
```


</details>
